truee
did you take 70
oh
have you heard other people saying 70 was bad
I'm about to graduate and CS 70 is still by far the most difficult class I've ever taken. Some upper divs maybe have a higher workload but no other class has left me so confused and discouraged and unconfident in myself. I took it over the summer and struggled really badly and felt very depressed. I straight up got 33% on the final.
I think to succeed in CS 70 you have to have a really good study group and/or constantly be at office hours, and in addition you just have to be good at a certain way of thinking (in my opinion at least, since my brain just does not gel with that material at all).
However, please don't be discouraged about the rest of the CS major. Unless you're going heavily into theory classes (the 170 series), the most similar class you're going to have to take is CS 170. While 170 is difficult and theory heavy, I found it easier than 70 and its concepts to be much more engaging and tangible than most of 70. Proofs and probability are the most important takeaways from 70 and (from my more systems-heavy experience) they don't really show up that often in most CS upper divs, and if they do, it's much less rigorous.
Just do your best and stick it out for the rest of the semester. Ask a lot of questions in Zoom office hours, make sure you've reviewed everything, and go through a couple practice exams. If you get stuck then just try to understand the solutions (sorry I can't really give good advice because I ate shit in that class lmao). CS 70 caused great pain to me as it's doing to you right now, but I promise you that you'll find a lot to love in the CS upper divs.

Loved “AI 강의

스탠포드가 $200,000 AI 학위를 무료로 풀었다고 합니다

PR용 입문 강의가 아닙니다. 프론티어 모델을 만드는 사람들이 실제로 듣는 커리큘럼입니다. Google Brain 창시자 Andrew Ng, ImageNet을 만든 Fei-Fei Li, Jeff Dean이 "학생이었으면 좋겠다"고 언급한 Percy Liang까지. AI 역사를 쓴 사람들이 직접 가르칩니다.

1. 어떤 강의들이 공개되어 있을까요?

[CS230: Deep Learning] 딥러닝의 기초입니다. CNN, RNN, LSTM부터 BatchNorm, Dropout까지. 자율주행, 헬스케어, 음악 생성 등 실제 사례로 배웁니다. Andrew Ng가 직접 강의합니다.
[CME295: Transformers & LLMs] 트랜스포머 아키텍처의 핵심을 다룹니다. 어텐션 메커니즘부터 SFT, LoRA, RLHF까지. LLM을 실무에 적용하려면 여기서 시작하면 됩니다.
[CS336: Language Models from Scratch] LLM을 처음부터 끝까지 직접 만듭니다. 데이터 수집, 토크나이저, 트랜스포머 구현, 학습, 평가까지 전 과정을 코딩합니다. Jeff Dean이 "학생이었으면 좋겠다"고 말한 강의입니다.
[CS329H: ML from Human Feedback] ChatGPT를 ChatGPT답게 만드는 기술입니다. RLHF, DPO, 보상 모델링 등 인간 선호도 학습의 이론과 구현을 다룹니다.
[CS231N: Computer Vision] 컴퓨터 비전의 바이블입니다. ImageNet을 만든 Fei-Fei Li가 가르칩니다. 이미지 분류부터 객체 탐지, 생성 모델까지.
[CME295: LLM Evaluation & Scaling] 모델을 만드는 것과 평가하는 것은 다른 문제입니다. 벤치마크 설계, 스케일링 법칙, 실제 성능 측정 방법을 배웁니다.

Deep Learning (CS230): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rNRRGdS0rBbXOUGA0wjdh1X

Transformers & LLMs (CME295): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rPZxxeUFvQHCkZJsaEBdDZj

Language Models from Scratch (CS336): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rOY23Y0BoGoBGgQ1zmU_MT_

ML from Human Feedback (CS329H): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rNm525zyAObP4al43WAifZz

Computer Vision (CS231N): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rOmsNzYBMe0gJY2XS8AQg16

LLM Evaluation & Scaling (CME295): https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLoROMvodv4rObv1FMizXqumgVVdzX4_05”
